      2*m2^2*m3^2*m4^2*m5^2*t^2 + m2^2*m4^4*m5^2*t^2 + m1^2*m2^2*m5^4*t^2 - 
      m2^4*m5^4*t^2 + m2^2*m3^2*m5^4*t^2 - m2^2*m4^2*m5^4*t^2 + 
      m1^2*m2^4*t^3 - 2*m1^2*m2^2*m3^2*t^3 + m1^2*m3^4*t^3 - m2^4*m4^2*t^3 + 
      2*m2^2*m3^2*m4^2*t^3 - m3^4*m4^2*t^3 - 2*m2^4*m5^2*t^3 + 
      2*m1^2*m3^2*m5^2*t^3 + 2*m2^2*m3^2*m5^2*t^3 - 2*m2^2*m4^2*m5^2*t^3 + 
      m2^2*m5^4*t^3 + m3^2*m5^4*t^3 + m2^2*m5^2*t^4 - m3^2*m5^2*t^4 - 
      2*m1^6*m3^6*x3 + 4*m1^4*m2^2*m3^6*x3 - 2*m1^2*m2^4*m3^6*x3 - 
      2*m1^4*m3^8*x3 + 2*m1^2*m2^2*m3^8*x3 + 2*m1^6*m3^4*m4^2*x3 - 
      2*m1^4*m2^2*m3^4*m4^2*x3 - 2*m1^2*m2^4*m3^4*m4^2*x3 + 
      2*m2^6*m3^4*m4^2*x3 + 4*m1^4*m3^6*m4^2*x3 - 2*m1^2*m2^2*m3^6*m4^2*x3 - 
      2*m2^4*m3^6*m4^2*x3 - 2*m1^4*m2^2*m3^2*m4^4*x3 + 
      4*m1^2*m2^4*m3^2*m4^4*x3 - 2*m2^6*m3^2*m4^4*x3 - 2*m1^4*m3^4*m4^4*x3 - 
      2*m1^2*m2^2*m3^4*m4^4*x3 + 4*m2^4*m3^4*m4^4*x3 + 
      2*m1^2*m2^2*m3^2*m4^6*x3 - 2*m2^4*m3^2*m4^6*x3 + 2*m1^4*m3^6*m5^2*x3 - 
      4*m1^2*m2^2*m3^6*m5^2*x3 + 2*m2^4*m3^6*m5^2*x3 - 
      4*m1^4*m3^4*m4^2*m5^2*x3 + 8*m1^2*m2^2*m3^4*m4^2*m5^2*x3 - 
      4*m2^4*m3^4*m4^2*m5^2*x3 + 2*m1^4*m3^2*m4^4*m5^2*x3 - 
      4*m1^2*m2^2*m3^2*m4^4*m5^2*x3 + 2*m2^4*m3^2*m4^4*m5^2*x3 - 
      m1^6*m2^2*m3^2*t*x3 + 2*m1^4*m2^4*m3^2*t*x3 - m1^2*m2^6*m3^2*t*x3 + 
      m1^6*m3^4*t*x3 - 6*m1^4*m2^2*m3^4*t*x3 + 5*m1^2*m2^4*m3^4*t*x3 + 
      6*m1^4*m3^6*t*x3 - 6*m1^2*m2^2*m3^6*t*x3 + 2*m1^2*m3^8*t*x3 + 
      5*m1^4*m2^2*m3^2*m4^2*t*x3 - 6*m1^2*m2^4*m3^2*m4^2*t*x3 + 
      m2^6*m3^2*m4^2*t*x3 - 3*m1^4*m3^4*m4^2*t*x3 + 6*m1^2*m2^2*m3^4*m4^2*t*
       x3 - 3*m2^4*m3^4*m4^2*t*x3 - 4*m1^2*m3^6*m4^2*t*x3 + 
      2*m2^2*m3^6*m4^2*t*x3 - 6*m1^2*m2^2*m3^2*m4^4*t*x3 + 
      6*m2^4*m3^2*m4^4*t*x3 + 2*m1^2*m3^4*m4^4*t*x3 - 4*m2^2*m3^4*m4^4*t*x3 + 
      2*m2^2*m3^2*m4^6*t*x3 + m1^6*m3^2*m5^2*t*x3 - m1^4*m2^2*m3^2*m5^2*t*
       x3 - m1^2*m2^4*m3^2*m5^2*t*x3 + m2^6*m3^2*m5^2*t*x3 + 
      m1^4*m3^4*m5^2*t*x3 + 2*m1^2*m2^2*m3^4*m5^2*t*x3 - 
      3*m2^4*m3^4*m5^2*t*x3 - 2*m1^2*m3^6*m5^2*t*x3 - 2*m2^2*m3^6*m5^2*t*x3 - 
      3*m1^4*m3^2*m4^2*m5^2*t*x3 + 2*m1^2*m2^2*m3^2*m4^2*m5^2*t*x3 + 
      m2^4*m3^2*m4^2*m5^2*t*x3 + 4*m1^2*m3^4*m4^2*m5^2*t*x3 + 
      4*m2^2*m3^4*m4^2*m5^2*t*x3 - 2*m1^2*m3^2*m4^4*m5^2*t*x3 - 
      2*m2^2*m3^2*m4^4*m5^2*t*x3 - m1^4*m3^2*m5^4*t*x3 + 
      2*m1^2*m2^2*m3^2*m5^4*t*x3 - m2^4*m3^2*m5^4*t*x3 - 4*m1^4*m3^4*t^2*x3 + 
      4*m1^2*m2^2*m3^4*t^2*x3 - 4*m1^2*m3^6*t^2*x3 + 
      4*m1^2*m2^2*m3^2*m4^2*t^2*x3 - 4*m2^4*m3^2*m4^2*t^2*x3 +

      4*m2^2*m3^2*m4^4*t^2*x3 - 2*m1^4*m3^2*m5^2*t^2*x3 + 
      4*m1^2*m2^2*m3^2*m5^2*t^2*x3 - 2*m2^4*m3^2*m5^2*t^2*x3 -

      2*m1^2*m3^2*m4^2*m5^2*t^2*x3 - 2*m2^2*m3^2*m4^2*m5^2*t^2*x3 - 
      3*m1^2*m2^2*m3^2*t^3*x3 + 3*m1^2*m3^4*t^3*x3 + 
      3*m2^2*m3^2*m4^2*t^3*x3 - 3*m3^4*m4^2*t^3*x3 + 
      3*m1^2*m3^2*m5^2*t^3*x3 + 3*m2^2*m3^2*m5^2*t^3*x3 + m3^4*m5^2*t^3*x3 + 
      m3^2*m4^2*m5^2*t^3*x3 + m3^2*m5^4*t^3*x3 - 2*m3^2*m5^2*t^4*x3 - 
      m1^6*m3^6*x3^2 + 2*m1^4*m2^2*m3^6*x3^2 - m1^2*m2^4*m3^6*x3^2 - 
      m1^4*m3^8*x3^2 + m1^2*m2^2*m3^8*x3^2 + m1^6*m3^4*m4^2*x3^2 - 
      m1^4*m2^2*m3^4*m4^2*x3^2 - m1^2*m2^4*m3^4*m4^2*x3^2 + 
      m2^6*m3^4*m4^2*x3^2 + 2*m1^4*m3^6*m4^2*x3^2 - m1^2*m2^2*m3^6*m4^2*
       x3^2 - m2^4*m3^6*m4^2*x3^2 - m1^4*m2^2*m3^2*m4^4*x3^2 + 
      2*m1^2*m2^4*m3^2*m4^4*x3^2 - m2^6*m3^2*m4^4*x3^2 - 
      m1^4*m3^4*m4^4*x3^2 - m1^2*m2^2*m3^4*m4^4*x3^2 + 
      2*m2^4*m3^4*m4^4*x3^2 + m1^2*m2^2*m3^2*m4^6*x3^2 - 
      m2^4*m3^2*m4^6*x3^2 + m1^4*m3^6*m5^2*x3^2 - 2*m1^2*m2^2*m3^6*m5^2*
       x3^2 + m2^4*m3^6*m5^2*x3^2 - 2*m1^4*m3^4*m4^2*m5^2*x3^2 +

      m2^4*m3^2*m4^4*m5^2*x3^2 + m1^6*m3^4*t*x3^2 - 2*m1^4*m2^2*m3^4*t*x3^2 + 
      m1^2*m2^4*m3^4*t*x3^2 + 4*m1^4*m3^6*t*x3^2 - 2*m1^2*m2^2*m3^6*t*x3^2 +

      2*m1^4*m3^4*m4^2*t*x3^2 - 2*m2^4*m3^4*m4^2*t*x3^2 - 
      2*m1^2*m3^6*m4^2*t*x3^2 + m2^2*m3^6*m4^2*t*x3^2 - 
      2*m1^2*m2^2*m3^2*m4^4*t*x3^2 + 4*m2^4*m3^2*m4^4*t*x3^2 + 
      m1^2*m3^4*m4^4*t*x3^2 - 2*m2^2*m3^4*m4^4*t*x3^2 + 
      m2^2*m3^2*m4^6*t*x3^2 - m1^4*m3^4*m5^2*t*x3^2 + 
      2*m1^2*m2^2*m3^4*m5^2*t*x3^2 - m2^4*m3^4*m5^2*t*x3^2 - 
      m1^2*m3^6*m5^2*t*x3^2 - m2^2*m3^6*m5^2*t*x3^2 - 
      m1^4*m3^2*m4^2*m5^2*t*x3^2 + 2*m1^2*m2^2*m3^2*m4^2*m5^2*t*x3^2 - 
      m2^4*m3^2*m4^2*m5^2*t*x3^2 + 2*m1^2*m3^4*m4^2*m5^2*t*x3^2 + 
      2*m2^2*m3^4*m4^2*m5^2*t*x3^2 - m1^2*m3^2*m4^4*m5^2*t*x3^2 - 
      m2^2*m3^2*m4^4*m5^2*t*x3^2 - 3*m1^4*m3^4*t^2*x3^2 + 
      3*m1^2*m2^2*m3^4*t^2*x3^2 - 3*m1^2*m3^6*t^2*x3^2 + 
      3*m1^2*m2^2*m3^2*m4^2*t^2*x3^2 - 3*m2^4*m3^2*m4^2*t^2*x3^2 + 
      3*m1^2*m3^4*m4^2*t^2*x3^2 + 3*m2^2*m3^4*m4^2*t^2*x3^2 - 
      3*m2^2*m3^2*m4^4*t^2*x3^2 - 2*m1^2*m2^2*m3^2*t^3*x3^2 + 
      2*m1^2*m3^4*t^3*x3^2 + 2*m2^2*m3^2*m4^2*t^3*x3^2 - 
      2*m3^4*m4^2*t^3*x3^2 + m1^2*m3^2*m5^2*t^3*x3^2 + 
      m2^2*m3^2*m5^2*t^3*x3^2 + m3^4*m5^2*t^3*x3^2 + 
      m3^2*m4^2*m5^2*t^3*x3^2 - m3^2*m5^2*t^4*x3^2)/
     ((m3^2 - m4^2 + t)*(m1^4 - 2*m1^2*m2^2 + m2^4 - 2*m1^2*t - 2*m2^2*t + 
       t^2)*(m1^4*m3^2 - m1^2*m2^2*m3^2 + m1^2*m3^4 - m1^2*m2^2*m4^2 + 
       m2^4*m4^2 - m1^2*m3^2*m4^2 - m2^2*m3^2*m4^2 + m2^2*m4^4 - 
       m1^2*m3^2*m5^2 + m2^2*m3^2*m5^2 + m1^2*m4^2*m5^2 - m2^2*m4^2*m5^2 + 
       m1^2*m2^2*t - m1^2*m3^2*t - m2^2*m4^2*t + m3^2*m4^2*t - m1^2*m5^2*t - 
       m2^2*m5^2*t - m3^2*m5^2*t - m4^2*m5^2*t + m5^4*t + m5^2*t^2)*
      (x1 + x2 + x3 + x1*x3 + x2*x3)*(m5^2*x1 + m5^2*x2 - t*x1*x2 + m5^2*x3 + 
       m3^2*x1*x3 + m5^2*x1*x3 - t*x1*x3 + m3^2*x2*x3 + m5^2*x2*x3 - 
       t*x1*x2*x3 + m3^2*x3^2 + m3^2*x1*x3^2 + m3^2*x2*x3^2 + 
       m1^2*x1*(x1 + x2 + x3 + x1*x3 + x2*x3) + 
       m2^2*x2*(x1 + x2 + x3 + x1*x3 + x2*x3)))
